### 1. Core Tactical Guidance  
- **Strategy reminder:** “Big winners pay for small losers.”  
- **Symbol selection rule:**  
  - Prioritize symbols with **high `avg_win`** and **high `total_pnl`** (large historical winners).  
  - **Avoid** symbols that have incurred **3+ losses** (repeat losers).  
  - **Never** clip winners early or add to a blocked position.

- **Total symbols tracked:** ~100+.  
- **Wins:** **0** across the entire data set (no winning trade recorded).  
- **Losses:** Thousands of small losses; average loss per trade ≈ **0.0005 USDT** (≈0.05 % of a 1‑USDT position).  
- **Largest cumulative loss:** `RESOLV‑USDT` with **‑0.3389 USDT** (5 losses).  
- **Most blocked symbols:** `Q‑USDT` (11 blocks), `VELVET‑USDT` (1 block), `AVAAI‑USDT` (3 blocks), `POPCAT‑USDT` (4 blocks).  

---

### 5. Key Insights & Actionable Points  

1. **No winning trades yet** – the system is still in a loss‑recovery phase.  
2. **Focus on symbols that have shown any positive total PnL** (even if tiny) and **low block counts**. Currently the only candidates are the handful listed in the “Top‑ranked” table.  
3. **Avoid re‑entering** any symbol that already has **≥3 losses** (e.g., `RESOLV‑USDT`, `DRIFT‑USDT`, `SAGA‑USDT`).  
4. **Do not clip** the few positions that may move toward the TP; the TP levels are already set (e.g., GOAT‑USDT TP 0.01460).  
5. **Consider adjusting position size** to stay within the tight stop loss window (≈1 % of entry) to keep losses small and fast, per the Profit Doctrine.  

---

### 6. Errors / Issues Detected  

- **All recent trades hit stop‑losses**; no TP was reached, indicating possible over‑aggressive TP placement or market conditions not supporting the expected momentum.  
- Several symbols are **blocked** (e.g., `VELVET‑USDT`, `AVAAI‑USDT`, `POPCAT‑USDT`) – attempting to trade them will be rejected by the engine.  
- **Zero win count** suggests the current entry criteria may be too loose or the market is currently unfavorable; a review of the entry filter (volume, volatility, 24 h move) is warranted.  

---

### 7. Recommended Next Steps  

1. **Filter candidate list** to symbols with:  
   - `total_pnl ≥ 0` (or the least negative).  
   - `blocked ≤ 1`.  
   - **No more than 2 historical losses**.  

2. **Re‑evaluate TP levels** for the most recent entries (e.g., GOAT‑USDT, STABLE‑USDT) to ensure the 3.6 %+ target is realistic given current volatility.  

3. **Maintain tight stop‑losses** (≈1 % of entry) to keep losers “small and fast.”  

4. **Log each trade** with orderId verification (must appear in `trade_journal.jsonl`) to avoid phantom‑execution errors.  

---  

*This summary captures the most relevant data for adjusting the next trading cycle while respecting the non‑negotiable Profit Doctrine.*
